de cookies</h2><p id="awsccc-cb-text"><span>Utilizamos cookies esenciales y herramientas similares que son necesarias para suministrar tanto nuestro sitio como nuestros servicios. Utilizamos cookies de rendimiento a fin de recopilar estadísticas anónimas y así comprender la forma en que los clientes utilizan nuestro sitio con el objetivo de realizar mejoras. Las cookies esenciales no se pueden desactivar, pero puede hacer clic en “Personalizar cookies” para rechazar las cookies de rendimiento. <br><br> Si está de acuerdo, AWS y terceros autorizados también utilizarán cookies para suministrar características útiles del sitio, recordar las preferencias y mostrar contenido relevante, incluida publicidad pertinente. Para continuar sin aceptar estas cookies, haga clic en “Continuar sin aceptar”. Por lo general, solo se emplean en respuesta a las acciones que lleve a cabo en el sitio, por ejemplo, al configurar sus preferencias de privacidad, al iniciar sesión o al completar formularios. </p></div><div class="awsccc-cs-s-action"></div></div><div data-category="performance" class="awsccc-cs-s-container"><h3 class="awsccc-cs-s-title">De rendimiento</h3><div class="awsccc-cs-s-text"><p class="awsccc-cs-s-paragraph">Las cookies de rendimiento proporcionan estadísticas anónimas sobre la forma en que los clientes navegan por nuestro sitio para que podamos mejorar la experiencia y el rendimiento del sitio. Los terceros aprobados pueden realizar análisis en nuestro nombre, pero no pueden utilizar los datos para sus propios fines.</p></div><div class="awsccc-cs-s-action"><div><div class="awsccc-cs-s-cb-outer"><div class="awscc-u-cb-checkbox-container" data-id="awsccc-u-cb-performance-container"><label data-id="awsccc-u-cb-performance-label" class="awsccc-u-cb-label awsccc-u-cb-checkbox-active"><input id="awsccc-u-cb-performance" class="awsccc-u-cb-input" type="checkbox" aria-checked="true" checked=""><span class="awsccc-cs-s-cb-hidden">Permitir categoría de rendimiento</span><svg viewBox="0 0 14 14" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="awscc-u-cb-checkbox"><rect class="awscc-u-cb-checkbox-rect" x="0.5" y="0.5" rx="1.5" ry="1.5" width="13" height="13"></rect><polyline class="awscc-u-cb-checkbox-poly-line " points="2.5,7 6,10 11,3"></polyline></svg></label></div></div><span class="awsccc-u-cb-text">Permitidas</span></div></div></div><div data-category="functional" class="awsccc-cs-s-container"><h3 class="awsccc-cs-s-title">Funcionales</h3><div class="awsccc-cs-s-text"><p class="awsccc-cs-s-paragraph">Las cookies funcionales nos ayudan a proporcionar características útiles del sitio, recordar sus preferencias y mostrar contenido relevante. The defaults are still quite aggressive, but can be changed with cvar. Check out e_MergedMeshesLodRatio and e_MergedMeshesViewDistRatio to control total distance that merged mesh vegetation renders and where the quality starts to drop off. Also e_MergedMeshesInstanceDistShadows controls how far away to render shadows on merged mesh vegetation. User should be able to make things much better by tweaking some values, at least in the latest version of LY.*\n\nHope this helps!","upvoteCount":0,"url":"https://repost.aws/questions/QUndEqT6iPSvSLRQOw38r9Ow/1-6-problem-with-vegetation-applied-via-terrain-layers#AN-G3pOQHCToif3j4LfwtU8Q"},{"@type":"Answer","text":"Thanks for the video. class="custom-md-style"><p>I am attempting to create vegetation variation by using the Terrain Layers to distribute groups of vegetation. I am running into what seems to be an LOD issue with this method. Initially I thought it to be one of two things, a texture LOD issue, or a terrain LOD issue. I believe I have eliminated these as a cause and am at this point completely stumped. I've dug through the cvars to find every possible variable and spent hours trying to find it but was unsuccessful. I did find the two vars I thought might fix it but here is the video to demonstrate the results.</p>
<p>Starts out with e_TerrainLodRatio at 0. Switch "Detail layer view distance" in Environment from default to 0, then to 100. Switch e_TerrainLodRatio back to default (0.5).</p>
<p><a href="https://youtu.be/yE1XhLN4Fmw" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" aria-label="https://youtu.be/yE1XhLN4Fmw youtu" target="_blank">https://youtu.be/yE1XhLN4Fmw</a></p>
<p>I realize this is not the recommended method to distribute vegetation, but this is the most logical for the number of plants I want to distribute and the uniformity of the distribution over multiple varying areas.</p>
<p>I believe this behavior can be replicated easily with any project/level.</p>

CustomTag_tag__AFOoQ CustomTag_accepted__rw0fi">Respuesta aceptada</span></div></div><div class="custom-md-style"><p>This problem is directly related to the e_ProcVegetationMaxSectorsInCache system variable, which must be set in either the game.cfg or the system<!-- -->&lt;platform&gt;<!-- -->.cfg file. Just add a line like this:</p>
<pre><code>e_ProcVegetationMaxSectorsInCache=64
</code></pre>
<p>This setting requires an editor restart, which is why changing the value in the editor doesn't show any change.</p>

class="custom-md-style"><p>Ok, after some further digging through the code, it appears as if this issue is related to the cached sectors that the procedural objects are using. It seems that the cvar e_ProcVegetationMaxSectorsInCache can't be changed, which doesn't allow for any more sectors to be allocated. FYI there is a debug mode for the procedural vegetation e_ProcVegetation = 2:</p>
<p>REMOVEDUPLOAD</p>
<p>REMOVEDUPLOAD</p>
<p>EDIT: Changing this cvar requires a restart, so it must be set in either the game.cfg or the system*.cfg. SOLVED!</p></div><div class="AnswerView_userActionContainer__l9bpb"><div class="AnswerView_actionContainer__v9led"><button title="Compartir" data-test="share-btn" type="button" class="ant-btn AnswerView_tags__4tTFf"></div><div class="custom-md-style"><p>Hi all, I have some new info from one of our engineers:
<em>I made some improvements a few months back to how merged mesh vegetation LOD'd out over distance. The defaults are still quite aggressive, but can be changed with cvar. Check out e_MergedMeshesLodRatio and e_MergedMeshesViewDistRatio to control total distance that merged mesh vegetation renders and where the quality starts to drop off. Also e_MergedMeshesInstanceDistShadows controls how far away to render shadows on merged mesh vegetation. User should be able to make things much better by tweaking some values, at least in the latest version of LY.</em></p>
<p>Hope this helps!</p></div><div class="AnswerView_userActionContainer__l9bpb"><div class="AnswerView_actionContainer__v9led"><button title="Compartir" data-test="share-btn" type="button"
